 echo "#"; LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/tmp/postfix/src/postfix-3.0.3/lib LD_LIBRARY_PATH=/tmp/postfix/src/postfix-3.0.3/lib ./postconf -d -c ../../conf) | \
    egrep -v '^(myhostname|mydomain|mynetworks|process_name|process_id) ' >../../conf/main.cf.default
